false, nil\n}\n\nfunc matchesBool(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) (bool, error) {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase flipt.OpNotPresent:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) == 0, nil\n\tcase flipt.OpPresent:\n\t\treturn len(strings.TrimSpace(v)) != 0, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// can't parse an empty string\n\tif v == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvalue, err := strconv.ParseBool(v)\n\tif Find the import block\n            import_match = re.search(r'import\\s*\\((.*?)\\)', content, re.DOTALL)\n            if import_match:\n                import_block = import_match.group(1)\n                # Find all import paths\n                imports = re.findall(r'\"([^\"]+)\"', import_block)\n                for imp in imports:\n                    stripped = strip_module_prefix(imp)\n                    if stripped:\n                        internal_imports.append(stripped)\n            #
